## Motivation factors


::: {.cell}
::: {.cell-output-display}
|**Characteristic**         | **N = 171** |
|:--------------------------|:-----------:|
|To make money              |             |
|large extent               |  126 (74%)  |
|no extent                  |  3 (1.8%)   |
|small extent               |  42 (25%)   |
|To remove boredom          |             |
|large extent               |  51 (30%)   |
|no extent                  |  71 (42%)   |
|small extent               |  49 (29%)   |
|To relieve stress          |             |
|large extent               |  61 (36%)   |
|no extent                  |  39 (23%)   |
|small extent               |  71 (42%)   |
|for socialization          |             |
|large extent               |  105 (61%)  |
|no extent                  |  21 (12%)   |
|small extent               |  45 (26%)   |
|for recreation             |             |
|large extent               |  40 (23%)   |
|no extent                  |  26 (15%)   |
|small extent               |  105 (61%)  |
|lack of self control       |             |
|large extent               |  19 (11%)   |
|no extent                  |  46 (27%)   |
|small extent               |  105 (62%)  |
|Unknown                    |      1      |
|Easy accesibility of sites |             |
|large extent               |  74 (43%)   |
|no extent                  |  22 (13%)   |
|small extent               |  75 (44%)   |
|for fun and excitement     |             |
|large extent               |  44 (26%)   |
|small extent               |  127 (74%)  |
:::
